<gmap_id>0x808fddbd319b6d7d:0xb7c97572160235d5< /gmap_id></record>

<Rating>4<//Rating><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNUQtOQiGXO-UfEF8gYqU9yLbFB2Twhqgyi3ZBf=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO4qZkY0qlxFmsToB-d-_xCQrIeiCQi9CyD79R9=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pics><time>1610134439010< /time>< Text>
It's a great walking park with sites of wine production, gnarled oaks, and Livermore's best spring flowers. The park has a divided bike/walking asphalt trail and two other hills you can walk up and around. There is a great shot at the top of the hills of Livermore Valley and Mount Diablo. Parking is at the top of the entrance past the farmer :)

Estimated walk time: 30-85 minutes depending if you go on the back trail and if you are going slow.</Text>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
Jobspring has treated me very well both in front of and behind the interviewing table.  They have a consistent, professional demeanor about them and are extremely meticulous about selecting people who are the right fit for prospective positions.

I was first introduced to Jobspring during my time as a software engineering manager.  Brian placed excellent candidates who were not only technically proficient, but were also great culture fits.  Every candidate came in highly-motivated and ready to work hard, and their continuing thirst for excellence helped each of them go on to do great things with my team.  We never had a bad hire through Jobspring.

Later, when I began seeking new opportunities, I went to Jobspring for my job-seeking needs.  My experience has been excellent.  From the other side of the table, Brian and Kyle were both professional, empathetic, and ultimately concerned with placing me in a position where I could not only earn a competitive salary, but where I could thrive professionally and personally.  They worked with me to refine my interviewing skills, briefed me before each interview, debriefed me after each interview, and walked me through the process of determining whether each place was truly the right fit for me.  I credit their meticulousness for both helping me avoid loose fits and landing me the right position.

I start my new opportunity in the next couple weeks, and I have Jobspring Partners to thank for that.  Thank you, Brian and Kyle: you're doing great work!<//Review>

< Review>
I've worked with Jobspring twice now and both times I've been extremely happy with their service.  The first time with Brian, and the second with Brian and Kyle.

They really take their time to try to know their candidates and build a relationship with them.  They genuinely want what's best for their candidate and they don't pressure them into into just taking any job just so Jobspring can get paid.  When I most recently worked with them, I ended up accepting an offer I found on my own.  They were very understanding and told me I should do what's best for my career.

Although the recruiters at Jobspring don't have a technical background, they do try to learn as much about the tech world as possible.  They're very knowledgeable about all the different technologies the industry is using right now, and have some understanding on what those technologies do.  Some of them have even admitted to taking online programming classes.  I really appreciate this.  Not only does this allow them to have more informed conversations when trying to match up candidates with companies, but it also seems like they really try to relate  to and understand their candidates.

Overall, Jobspring recruiters are very friendly, professional, understanding, and  genuinely invested in your career.  I intended to work with them every time I need a change in my career.<//Review>

< Review>
I gave them my resume on a Sunday, I had several first round interviews over the phone the first week, and then had in person interviews the following.  I got a verbal offer within 48 hours from the company I liked the best.  These guys are intense, they work as a fantastic team and you're part of the process the whole way.
This place is not a resume black hole, it's a real amazing set of very knowledgeable and connected people that just want to help you.
You should judge a recruiter based on a number of factors. Firstly, they need to be able to get the job done - they need to get you in front of potential employers.  Jobspring has outdone every recruiter I've ever used in terms of raw interviews.  You don't just have one guy working your resume around, they put a team on it.  It's intense: you're going to talk to a number of people about yourself and they are going to make the magic happen. (In fact, stop talking to recruiters that can't present your resume well enough to get an interview.  Use someone better)
Secondly, you should judge their ability to help you prepare for the interview by getting you an understanding of the company.  They excel at this, and they excel at supporting you through the very emotionally trying experience that a career search really is.
Expect to be a little overwhelmed and a bit taken back by their process at first.  However, trust these guys. They really go all in!
During the offer waiting process they kept me continuously up to date and made me understand the salary range that was expected from interview feedback.  They were professional and no-nonsense about it.  Incredible experience overall.
They actively are trying to enrich the interview experience for the companies they work with for the benefit of all.  That's just amazing.</Review>

< Text>
Very cute little venue and concept for a place, but location really blows for the vibes that they have going on.  I wish they had a larger space with off the street back patio outdoor seating rather then being right along the main drag of the street.

There is usually a line because they are good, so yeah.. deal with it.  When ordering for multiple people you will likely not get served up as you would a normal sit down restaurant.  They are a small venue and serve up in an efficient way that makes most sense for them.  If you want a real sit down and be served experience you should go to a sit down location.

Cutesy little names make this menu fun to mull over and it is most definitely a young eclectic group of people. I hope to return to try some more bites next time I am in the area.

Enjoy!< /Text>

<Text>I love the location of this small and local coffee shop/quick breakfast spot. Came this morning to grab some takeout for breakfast and decided to go with the Freakin French Toast. If you are craving for something sweet and somewhat heavy to start your day, Hippie's Brew is the way to go!

<Rating>4< /Rating><Review>I like Hippie Brew and my girlfriend loves them. Before Covid I would stop by here more often while doing work at the library. The staff has always been friendly, at every location current and former.

The only reason for the dropped star is that it does wear on me. The menu is limited, cold brew cocktails only. No espresso drinks. If that's your thing you can even buy a jug and make your own at home. I keep some on hand for my girlfriend, for sure.

So although I love their selection, some days they're just too sweet for me. I'd still recommend it to anyone who's seeking a good, local coffee spot. Better than St*rbuck's drinks, for sure. But if you're looking for a less sweet espresso drink, Hippie Brew wouldn't be the place to go.

< text>
Very popular, quirky local coffee shop with fun food options. Located in the Hayward Library building, with it's own entrance, allowing it to open outside of library hours. The only drip coffee option within reasonable distance of Hayward. Their drop coffee and chai tea drinks are fabulous! Definitely try "Ice Loves Coco" and "Yogi Chai".</text>

< text>
Creative and delicious drinks, made with fresh ingredients and a very welcoming staff. My only complaint is the over-familiarity within the staff. I understand playful banter, but a group of 3 or 4 was yelling over me as I was ordering, and I had to wait until they were finished yelling over me to finish my order. This is my second time here, and definitely won't be my last, as long as I have the time to wait the 10-15 minutes for my drinks (these times are based off when they got to start by drinks without anyone ahead of me). Sadly an experience like that takes away from what that have to offer, which is a beautiful ambiance  with a home-kitchen vibe.< /text>

< Review>
Exactly what the name of the place is. Once you step in, you get the feel of being in the 1960's. Baristas are very nice, they even offered me a free cookie. Coffee was different than what I'm used to. Try the mint leaf coffee. Overall, new experience and new atmosphere for a coffee shop. I'll definitely be stopping here more often. Only thing is that, sadly, the coffee shop is a bit hidden among other businesses. Also, a bit hard to see while driving, especially how fast the traffic flow is on Foothill Blvd.</Review>

< Review>
A spirited little place with lots of character, I chose it as a midway meeting point between Silicon Valley and Berkeley.  The  food menu is creative with simple ingredients, nice combinations and good preparation. The coffee menu is superb, I had the peppermint patty: medium roast (instead of dark) with cocoa powder (a bit like a mocha), with fresh peppermint, √° la mint tea, cream and sweet ground candy sprinkle! It was fantastic and I ended up ordering another one for the drive home!

Service is super friendly and the barista, the sandwich maker and the other guys working there are super friendly and chatty.

Overall the Hippie's Brew made for a very interesting meeting place and a pleasant lunch, coffee and ambient.  Will definitely stop by if going that way!</Review>

< text>
I had never heard of this place until my hair cut guy pointed it out. I went here for just the intent of grabbing a coffee, having a conversation for a few minutes and leave. That was done smoothly, and easily because there was not to many people inside this small building, and the coffee experts made the coffee in a good amount of time.

The drink selection took me a little while to pick from because there menu was just a little scattered for my liking but that doesn't mean I couldn't find something I wanted. I found multiple drinks I wanted and got feedback from the staff on what drink I would like the most.
Drink was fantastic and my friends drink was even better.

The only complaint is how small the building is, but you just have to get comfortable sitting close to people!

Would highly recommend this place if you want some great coffee!< /text>

< Review>
The good part of Rocklin Smiles is the pleasant and friendly atmosphere inside the building. Everyone is going out of their way to make you feel comfortable. The two stars however are an evaluation prompted by the actual work and its consequences. I went in just for a checkup with no pain or issues.  Dr Maasri stated that she detected a cavity and that the best solution would be a crown. We proceeded with the procedure but I was somewhat uneasy by the process; most of the actual crown work was done by an assistant (technician) and the post bite adjustment took maybe 5 minutes.  Dr. Maasri told me that I could come back for any issue. The pain over the next days was pretty substantial and grew to chronic pain into my lower and upper jaw reaching my cheekbone. When I started waking up at nights, I made a new appointment. During the second appointment new adjustment to my bite were done but again pain drove me to take ibuprofen for pain reduction and possible inflammation. After my third visit the bite was finally corrected as it should be and now I am pain free.
Again, the office is trying to be super friendly but the actual dentist work seems to be rushed in completion. My days and nights of pain could have been prevented by an extra 15-30 minutes of bite correction; it seems the dentist did not have the needed experience to identify and complete the bite correction properly.<//Review>
